--- Views\Orders\Checkout.cshtml ---
﻿@model ThriftLoop.ViewModels.CheckoutViewModel
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Confirm Purchase";
    Layout = null;

    string condClass = Model.ItemCondition switch
    {
        "New" => "detail-condition--new",
        "Like New" => "detail-condition--like-new",
        "Good" => "detail-condition--good",
        "Fair" => "detail-condition--fair",
        _ => "detail-condition--poor"
    };
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Orders.css" asp-append-version="true" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Navbar.css" asp-append-version="true" />
</head>
<body>
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Navbar")

    <div class="co-shell">

        @* ── Back navigation ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <nav class="co-breadcrumb" aria-label="Breadcrumb">
            @if (Model.IsShopOrder)
            {
                <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Shop" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                       class="co-breadcrumb__link">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" aria-hidden="true">
                        <path d="M12.5 5L7.5 10L12.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                    </svg>
                    Back to listing
                </a>
            }
            else
            {
                <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Items" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                       class="co-breadcrumb__link">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" aria-hidden="true">
                        <path d="M12.5 5L7.5 10L12.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                    </svg>
                    Back to listing
                </a>
            }
        </nav>

        <header class="co-header">
            <h1 class="co-header__title">
                @(Model.WasStolen ? "Complete Your Steal" : "Confirm Your Purchase")
            </h1>
            <p class="co-header__subtitle">
                @if (Model.WasStolen)
                {
                    @:You stole this item — complete checkout to secure it, or cancel to return it.
                }
                else
                {
                    @:Review the details below before finalising.
                }
            </p>
        </header>

        @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)
        {
            <div class="co-alert co-alert--error" role="alert">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-8-5a.75.75 0 01.75.75v4.5a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0v-4.5A.75.75 0 0110 5zm0 10a1 1 0 100-2 1 1 0 000 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
                @errMsg
                @if (errMsg.Contains("wallet") || errMsg.Contains("balance"))
                {
                    <a asp-action="AddFunds" asp-controller="Wallet" class="co-alert__link">Add funds →</a>
                }
            </div>
        }

        <div class="co-grid">

            @* ════════════ LEFT — Item summary ════════════ *@
            <div class="co-summary-col">

                <div class="co-item-card">
                    <div class="co-item-card__img-wrap">
                        @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.ItemImageUrl))
                        {
                            <img src="@Model.ItemImageUrl" alt="Photo of @Model.ItemTitle"
                                 class="co-item-card__img" loading="eager" />
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <div class="co-item-card__img co-item-card__img--placeholder" aria-hidden="true">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                    <rect x="6" y="10" width="52" height="44" rx="6" />
                                    <circle cx="22" cy="26" r="6" />
                                    <path d="M6 46l16-14 10 10 8-7 18 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                </svg>
                            </div>
                        }
                        @if (Model.IsStealable)
                        {
                            <span class="co-item-card__stealable-badge">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path d="M7.75 1.5L2.5 8h4.25L5.5 12.5 11.5 6H7.25L7.75 1.5z" />
                                </svg>
                                @(Model.WasStolen ? "Stolen" : "Stealable")
                            </span>
                        }
                    </div>

                    <div class="co-item-card__body">
                        <div class="co-item-card__meta">
                            <span class="co-item-card__category">@Model.ItemCategory</span>
                            <span class="co-item-card__condition @condClass">@Model.ItemCondition</span>

                            @* P2P: show item size if available *@
                            @if (!Model.IsShopOrder && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.ItemSize))
                            {
                                <span class="co-item-card__size">@Model.ItemSize</span>
                            }

                            @* Shop (Option B): show variant, size, and quantity chips *@
                            @if (Model.IsShopOrder)
                            {
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.SelectedVariantName) && Model.SelectedVariantName != "Default")
                                {
                                    <span class="co-item-card__size co-chip--shop">@Model.SelectedVariantName</span>
                                }
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.SelectedSize))
                                {
                                    <span class="co-item-card__size co-chip--shop">@Model.SelectedSize</span>
                                }
                                <span class="co-item-card__size co-chip--qty">×@Model.Quantity</span>
                            }
                        </div>

                        <h2 class="co-item-card__title">@Model.ItemTitle</h2>

                        <div class="co-item-card__seller">
                            <div class="co-item-card__seller-avatar" aria-hidden="true">
                                @char.ToUpper(Model.SellerName.FirstOrDefault())
                            </div>
                            <div>
                                <p class="co-item-card__seller-label">Sold by</p>
                                <p class="co-item-card__seller-name">@Model.SellerName</p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                @* ── Left-column notices ──────────────────────────────────────── *@
                @if (Model.WasStolen)
                {
                    <div class="co-cancel-steal-notice" role="note">
                        <div class="co-cancel-steal-notice__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">
                                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm-1-9a1 1 0 112 0v4a1 1 0 11-2 0V9zm1-4a1 1 0 100 2 1 1 0 000-2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                            </svg>
                        </div>
                        <div class="co-cancel-steal-notice__body">
                            <p class="co-cancel-steal-notice__heading">Changed your mind?</p>
                            <p class="co-cancel-steal-notice__text">
                                You can cancel the steal — the ₱50 premium is removed and the item returns to available for anyone to claim.
                            </p>
                            <form asp-action="CancelSteal" asp-controller="Items"
                                  asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId" method="post" style="margin-top:10px">
                                @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                <button type="submit" class="co-cancel-steal-btn">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                        <path d="M6.28 5.22a.75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06L8.94 10l-3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 101.06 1.06L10 11.06l3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 101.06-1.06L11.06 10l3.72-3.72a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06L10 8.94 6.28 5.22z" />
                                    </svg>
                                    Cancel Steal &amp; Return Item
                                </button>
                            </form>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                }
                else if (Model.IsShopOrder)
                {
                    <div class="co-p2p-notice" role="note">
                        <div class="co-p2p-notice__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="20" height="20">
                                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a.75.75 0 000 1.5h.253a.25.25 0 01.244.304l-.459 2.066A1.75 1.75 0 0010.747 15H11a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-.253a.25.25 0 01-.244-.304l.459-2.066A1.75 1.75 0 009.253 9H9z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                            </svg>
                        </div>
                        <div class="co-p2p-notice__body">
                            <p class="co-p2p-notice__heading">Shop order</p>
                            <p class="co-p2p-notice__text">
                                You're purchasing from <strong>@Model.SellerName</strong>'s shop.
                                After confirming, coordinate for delivery or pick-up.
                            </p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                }
                else
                {
                    <div class="co-p2p-notice" role="note">
                        <div class="co-p2p-notice__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="20" height="20">
                                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a.75.75 0 000 1.5h.253a.25.25 0 01.244.304l-.459 2.066A1.75 1.75 0 0010.747 15H11a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-.253a.25.25 0 01-.244-.304l.459-2.066A1.75 1.75 0 009.253 9H9z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                            </svg>
                        </div>
                        <div class="co-p2p-notice__body">
                            <p class="co-p2p-notice__heading">This is a P2P transaction</p>
                            <p class="co-p2p-notice__text">
                                ThriftLoop connects buyers and sellers directly. After confirming,
                                coordinate with <strong>@Model.SellerName</strong> for pickup or shipping.
                            </p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                }

            </div>

            @* ════════════ RIGHT — Price breakdown + confirm ════════════ *@
            <div class="co-order-col">

                <div class="co-breakdown">

                    <h2 class="co-breakdown__heading">Order Summary</h2>

                    <div class="co-breakdown__rows">

                        @if (Model.IsShopOrder)
                        {
                            @* Shop order: show unit price, and if qty > 1 a subtotal row *@
                            <div class="co-breakdown__row">
                                <span class="co-breakdown__label">
                                    @Model.ItemTitle
                                    @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.SelectedVariantName) && Model.SelectedVariantName != "Default")
                                    {
                                        <text> — @Model.SelectedVariantName</text>
                                    }
                                    @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.SelectedSize))
                                    {
                                        <text> / @Model.SelectedSize</text>
                                    }
                                </span>
                                <span class="co-breakdown__value">₱@Model.BasePrice.ToString("N2")</span>
                            </div>

                            @if (Model.Quantity > 1)
                            {
                                <div class="co-breakdown__row co-breakdown__row--qty">
                                    <span class="co-breakdown__label co-breakdown__label--muted">
                                        Quantity
                                    </span>
                                    <span class="co-breakdown__value co-breakdown__value--muted">
                                        ×@Model.Quantity
                                    </span>
                                </div>
                            }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            @* P2P order: base price row *@
                            <div class="co-breakdown__row">
                                <span class="co-breakdown__label">
                                    @(Model.WasStolen ? "Base price" : Model.ItemTitle)
                                </span>
                                <span class="co-breakdown__value">₱@Model.BasePrice.ToString("N2")</span>
                            </div>

                            @if (Model.WasStolen)
                            {
                                <div class="co-breakdown__row co-breakdown__row--steal">
                                    <span class="co-breakdown__label">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="11" height="11"
                                             aria-hidden="true" class="co-breakdown__steal-icon">
                                            <path d="M7.75 1.5L2.5 8h4.25L5.5 12.5 11.5 6H7.25L7.75 1.5z" />
                                        </svg>
                                        Steal premium
                                    </span>
                                    <span class="co-breakdown__value co-breakdown__value--steal">
                                        +₱@Model.StealPremium.ToString("N2")
                                    </span>
                                </div>
                            }
                        }

                    </div>

                    @* ── Delivery fee row (only shown when Delivery is selected) ── *@
                    <div class="co-breakdown__row co-breakdown__row--delivery" id="deliveryFeeRow">
                        <span class="co-breakdown__label">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12" aria-hidden="true">
                                <path d="M3 3.5A1.5 1.5 0 014.5 2h7A1.5 1.5 0 0113 3.5v1a1 1 0 01-1 1H4a1 1 0 01-1-1v-1z" />
                                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M2 6.5A1.5 1.5 0 013.5 5h9A1.5 1.5 0 0114 6.5v6a1.5 1.5 0 01-1.5 1.5h-9A1.5 1.5 0 012 12.5v-6zM10 10a1 1 0 100 2 1 1 0 000-2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                            </svg>
                            Delivery Fee
                        </span>
                        <span class="co-breakdown__value" id="deliveryFeeValue">₱@Model.DeliveryFee.ToString("N2")</span>
                    </div>

                    <div class="co-breakdown__divider" aria-hidden="true"></div>

                    <div class="co-breakdown__total-row">
                        <span class="co-breakdown__total-label">Total</span>
                        <span class="co-breakdown__total-value" id="finalPriceDisplay">₱@Model.FinalPrice.ToString("N2")</span>
                    </div>

                    @* ── Fulfillment Method Selector ──────────────────────────────── *@
                    <div class="co-fulfillment-section">
                        <h3 class="co-fulfillment-section__heading">How would you like to receive this item?</h3>
                        
                        <div class="co-fulfillment-options" id="fulfillmentOptions">
                            @if (Model.AllowDelivery)
                            {
                                <label class="co-fulfillment-option @(Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod == "Delivery" ? "co-fulfillment-option--selected" : "")" data-method="Delivery">
                                    <input type="radio" name="fulfillmentMethod" value="Delivery" class="co-fulfillment-radio"
                                    @(Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod == "Delivery" ? "checked" : "") />
                                    <div class="co-fulfillment-option__content">
                                        <div class="co-fulfillment-option__icon">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="24" height="24">
                                                <path d="M4 7h16a2 2 0 012 2v8a2 2 0 01-2 2H4a2 2 0 01-2-2V9a2 2 0 012-2z" />
                                                <circle cx="7" cy="14" r="2" />
                                                <circle cx="17" cy="14" r="2" />
                                                <path d="M9 14h6" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="co-fulfillment-option__info">
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__title">Rider Delivery</span>
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__price">+₱@Model.DeliveryFee.ToString("N2") delivery fee</span>
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__description">A ThriftLoop rider will deliver this item. You'll pay the delivery fee to the rider in cash.</span>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </label>
                            }

                            @if (Model.AllowHalfway)
                            {
                                <label class="co-fulfillment-option @(Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod == "Halfway" ? "co-fulfillment-option--selected" : "")" data-method="Halfway">
                                    <input type="radio" name="fulfillmentMethod" value="Halfway" class="co-fulfillment-radio"
                                    @(Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod == "Halfway" ? "checked" : "") />
                                    <div class="co-fulfillment-option__content">
                                        <div class="co-fulfillment-option__icon">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="24" height="24">
                                                <path d="M12 2a7 7 0 00-7 7c0 5 7 13 7 13s7-8 7-13a7 7 0 00-7-7z" />
                                                <circle cx="12" cy="9" r="3" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="co-fulfillment-option__info">
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__title">Halfway Meetup</span>
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__price">No delivery fee</span>
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__description">Meet the seller at a halfway point. A chat will open after checkout to coordinate.</span>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </label>
                            }

                            @if (Model.AllowPickup)
                            {
                                <label class="co-fulfillment-option @(Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod == "Pickup" ? "co-fulfillment-option--selected" : "")" data-method="Pickup">
                                    <input type="radio" name="fulfillmentMethod" value="Pickup" class="co-fulfillment-radio"
                                    @(Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod == "Pickup" ? "checked" : "") />
                                    <div class="co-fulfillment-option__content">
                                        <div class="co-fulfillment-option__icon">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="24" height="24">
                                                <path d="M3 9l9-7 9 7v11a2 2 0 01-2 2H5a2 2 0 01-2-2V9z" />
                                                <path d="M9 22V12h6v10" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="co-fulfillment-option__info">
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__title">Self Pickup</span>
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__price">No delivery fee</span>
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__description">Pick up directly from the seller. A chat will open after checkout to arrange details.</span>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </label>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* ── Payment method selector ──────────────────────────────── *@
                    <div class="co-pay-section">
                        <h3 class="co-pay-section__heading">Payment method</h3>

                        <div class="co-pay-options" id="payOptions">

                            @* Wallet option *@
                            <label class="co-pay-option @(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "" : "co-pay-option--disabled")"
                                   id="payWalletLabel">
                                <input type="radio"
                                       name="paymentMethod"
                                       value="Wallet"
                                       class="co-pay-radio"
                                       id="payWallet"
                                @(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "checked" : "disabled") />
                                <div class="co-pay-option__icon">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16">
                                        <path d="M1 4.25a3.733 3.733 0 012-.575h13.5c.43 0 .845.069 1.232.198A2.25 2.25 0 0015.5 3h-11a3 3 0 00-3 3v1.25H1V4.25zM3.75 7A.75.75 0 013 6.25v-.5A2.75 2.75 0 015.75 3h8.5A2.75 2.75 0 0117 5.75v.5a.75.75 0 01-.75.75h-12.5z" />
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 8.5v6A2.5 2.5 0 003.5 17h13a2.5 2.5 0 002.5-2.5v-6A2.5 2.5 0 0016.5 6h-13A2.5 2.5 0 001 8.5zm14.5 3a1 1 0 100 2 1 1 0 000-2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                </div>
                                <div class="co-pay-option__body">
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__name">ThriftLoop Wallet</p>
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__detail">
                                        Balance: <strong>₱@Model.BuyerBalance.ToString("N2")</strong>
                                        @if (!Model.HasSufficientBalance)
                                        {
                                            <span class="co-pay-option__insufficient">
                                                — insufficient
                                                (<a asp-action="AddFunds" asp-controller="Wallet">add funds</a>)
                                            </span>
                                        }
                                        else
                                        {
                                            <text> · funds held in escrow until delivery</text>
                                        }
                                    </p>
                                </div>
                            </label>

                            @* Cash on Delivery option *@
                            <label class="co-pay-option" id="payCodLabel">
                                <input type="radio"
                                       name="paymentMethod"
                                       value="Cash"
                                       class="co-pay-radio"
                                       id="payCod"
                                @(!Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "checked" : "") />
                                <div class="co-pay-option__icon">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16">
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zM8.798 7.45c.512-.67 1.135-.95 1.702-.95s1.19.28 1.702.95a.75.75 0 001.192-.91C12.637 5.55 11.596 5 10.5 5s-2.137.55-2.894 1.54A4.501 4.501 0 007 9.5c0 1.079.37 2.077 1 2.879V14a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-1.734c-.35-.588-.5-1.14-.5-1.766 0-.863.275-1.61.798-2.05zM10 14.25a.75.75 0 100 1.5.75.75 0 000-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                </div>
                                <div class="co-pay-option__body">
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__name">Cash on Delivery / Meetup</p>
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__detail" id="cashPaymentDetail">Pay cash when your item arrives</p>
                                </div>
                            </label>

                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* ── Confirm form: routes to the right action based on order type ── *@
                    @if (Model.IsShopOrder)
                    {
                        <form asp-action="ConfirmShopOrder" asp-controller="Orders"
                              method="post" id="confirmForm">
                            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                            <input type="hidden" name="skuId" value="@Model.SkuId" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="quantity" value="@Model.Quantity" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="paymentMethod" id="paymentMethodInput"
                                   value="@(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "Wallet" : "Cash")" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="fulfillmentMethod" id="fulfillmentMethodInput"
                                   value="@Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod" />

                            <button type="submit" class="co-confirm-btn" id="confirmBtn">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                Confirm Purchase
                            </button>
                        </form>

                        <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Shop" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                               class="co-cancel-link">
                            Cancel and go back
                        </a>
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <form asp-action="ConfirmOrder" asp-controller="Orders"
                              method="post" id="confirmForm">
                            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                            <input type="hidden" name="itemId" value="@Model.ItemId" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="paymentMethod" id="paymentMethodInput"
                                   value="@(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "Wallet" : "Cash")" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="fulfillmentMethod" id="fulfillmentMethodInput"
                                   value="@Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod" />

                            <button type="submit" class="co-confirm-btn" id="confirmBtn">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                @(Model.WasStolen ? "Confirm Steal Purchase" : "Confirm Purchase")
                            </button>
                        </form>

                        @if (!Model.WasStolen)
                        {
                            <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Items" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                                   class="co-cancel-link">
                                Cancel and go back
                            </a>
                        }
                    }

                </div>

            </div>

        </div>

    </div>

    <script>
            (function () {
                'use strict';

                var paymentRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.co-pay-radio');
                var paymentHiddenInput = document.getElementById('paymentMethodInput');
                var fulfillmentRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.co-fulfillment-radio');
                var fulfillmentHiddenInput = document.getElementById('fulfillmentMethodInput');
                var form = document.getElementById('confirmForm');
                var btn = document.getElementById('confirmBtn');
                var deliveryFeeRow = document.getElementById('deliveryFeeRow');
                var deliveryFeeValue = document.getElementById('deliveryFeeValue');
                var finalPriceDisplay = document.getElementById('finalPriceDisplay');
                var cashPaymentDetail = document.getElementById('cashPaymentDetail');
                var fulfillmentOptions = document.querySelectorAll('.co-fulfillment-option');

                var basePrice = @Model.BasePrice;
                var stealPremium = @(Model.WasStolen? Model.StealPremium: 0);
                var deliveryFee = @Model.DeliveryFee;
                var quantity = @Model.Quantity;

                // Function to update UI based on selected fulfillment method
                function updateFulfillmentUI(method) {
                    var isDelivery = method === 'Delivery';
                
                    // Update option selection styling
                    fulfillmentOptions.forEach(function(opt) {
                        opt.classList.remove('co-fulfillment-option--selected');
                    });
                    var selectedOption = document.querySelector('.co-fulfillment-option[data-method="' + method + '"]');
                    if (selectedOption) {
                        selectedOption.classList.add('co-fulfillment-option--selected');
                    }
                
                    // Show/hide delivery fee row
                    if (deliveryFeeRow) {
                        deliveryFeeRow.style.display = isDelivery ? 'flex' : 'none';
                    }
                
                    // Calculate and update final price
                    var itemTotal = basePrice + stealPremium;
                    var finalPrice = isDelivery ? itemTotal + deliveryFee : itemTotal;
                
                    if (finalPriceDisplay) {
                        finalPriceDisplay.textContent = '₱' + finalPrice.toFixed(2).replace(/\d(?=(\d{3})+\.)/g, '$&,');
                    }
                
                    // Update cash payment detail text
                    if (cashPaymentDetail) {
                        if (isDelivery) {
                            cashPaymentDetail.textContent = 'Pay cash to the rider upon delivery';
                        } else if (method === 'Halfway') {
                            cashPaymentDetail.textContent = 'Pay cash to the seller when you meet';
                        } else if (method === 'Pickup') {
                            cashPaymentDetail.textContent = 'Pay cash to the seller when you pick up the item';
                        }
                    }
                
                    // Update hidden input
                    if (fulfillmentHiddenInput) {
                        fulfillmentHiddenInput.value = method;
                    }
                }

                // Keep payment method input in sync
                paymentRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                    radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                        if (paymentHiddenInput) paymentHiddenInput.value = radio.value;
                    });
                });

                // Handle fulfillment method selection
                fulfillmentRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                    radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                        updateFulfillmentUI(radio.value);
                    });
                });

                // Also handle click on the whole option card
                fulfillmentOptions.forEach(function(opt) {
                    opt.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        var radio = this.querySelector('.co-fulfillment-radio');
                        if (radio && !radio.disabled) {
                            radio.checked = true;
                            updateFulfillmentUI(radio.value);
                        }
                    });
                });

                // Initialize UI with default selection
                var checkedFulfillment = document.querySelector('.co-fulfillment-radio:checked');
                if (checkedFulfillment) {
                    updateFulfillmentUI(checkedFulfillment.value);
                } else {
                    // Default to first available option
                    var firstOption = document.querySelector('.co-fulfillment-radio');
                    if (firstOption) {
                        firstOption.checked = true;
                        updateFulfillmentUI(firstOption.value);
                    }
                }

                // Disable button + show spinner on submit
                if (form && btn) {
                    form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                        btn.disabled = true;
                        btn.innerHTML =
                            '<svg class="co-spin" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" ' +
                            'width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">' +
                            '<path d="M10 3a7 7 0 100 14A7 7 0 0010 3z" opacity=".3"/>' +
                            '<path d="M10 3a7 7 0 017 7h-1.5A5.5 5.5 0 0010 4.5V3z"/>' +
                            '</svg> Confirming\u2026';
                    });
                }

            }());
    </script>

    <style>
            /* Fulfillment Section Styles */
            .co-fulfillment-section {
                margin-top: 1.5rem;
                padding-top: 1rem;
                border-top: 1px solid var(--co-border, #e4e4ea);
            }

            .co-fulfillment-section__heading {
                font-size: 1rem;
                font-weight: 600;
                margin-bottom: 1rem;
                color: var(--co-text, #111827);
            }

            .co-fulfillment-options {
                display: flex;
                flex-direction: column;
                gap: 0.75rem;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option {
                cursor: pointer;
                display: block;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-radio {
                display: none;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option__content {
                display: flex;
                align-items: flex-start;
                gap: 1rem;
                padding: 1rem;
                border: 1.5px solid var(--co-border, #e4e4ea);
                border-radius: 12px;
                transition: all 0.15s;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option--selected .co-fulfillment-option__content,
            .co-fulfillment-radio:checked + .co-fulfillment-option__content {
                border-color: var(--co-primary, #2d1b69);
                background: rgba(45, 27, 105, 0.02);
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option__icon {
                flex-shrink: 0;
                color: #6b7280;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option--selected .co-fulfillment-option__icon,
            .co-fulfillment-radio:checked + .co-fulfillment-option__content .co-fulfillment-option__icon {
                color: var(--co-primary, #2d1b69);
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option__info {
                flex: 1;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option__title {
                display: block;

                margin-bottom: 0.25rem;

            .co-fulfillment-option__price {

            }

                color: #6b7280;

                .co-breakdown__row--delivery .co-breakdown__label {

            <div class="mp-empty">
                <div class="mp-empty__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                        <rect x="8" y="16" width="48" height="36" rx="6" />
                        <path d="M22 16v-4a10 10 0 0120 0v4" stroke-linecap="round" />
                        <path d="M24 36h16" stroke-linecap="round" />
                    </svg>
                </div>
                <h2 class="mp-empty__title">No purchases yet</h2>
                <p class="mp-empty__body">Items you confirm will appear here.</p>
                <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Home" class="btn btn--primary mp-empty__cta">
                    Browse listings
                </a>
            </div>
        }
        else
        {
            <div class="mp-list">
                @foreach (var order in Model)
                {
                    var sellerEmail = order.Seller?.Email ?? string.Empty;
                    var sellerDisplay = sellerEmail.Contains('@') ? sellerEmail.Split('@')[0] : sellerEmail;

                    string statusClass = order.Status switch
                    {
                        OrderStatus.Pending => "mp-status--pending",
                        OrderStatus.Completed => "mp-status--completed",
                        OrderStatus.Cancelled => "mp-status--cancelled",
                        _ => ""
                    };

                    string statusLabel = order.Status switch
                    {
                        OrderStatus.Pending => "Pending",
                        OrderStatus.Completed => "Completed",
                        OrderStatus.Cancelled => "Cancelled",
                        _ => order.Status.ToString()
                    };

                    string payLabel = order.PaymentMethod switch
                    {
                        PaymentMethod.Wallet => "Wallet (escrow)",
                        PaymentMethod.Cash => "Cash on Delivery",
                        _ => order.PaymentMethod.ToString()
                    };

                    // Check delivery status to determine if buyer can confirm receipt
                    bool canMarkDelivered = order.Status == OrderStatus.Pending
                        && order.Delivery != null
                        && order.Delivery.Status == DeliveryStatus.Delivered;
                    
                    // Show delivery status message
                    string deliveryStatusMessage = order.Delivery?.Status switch
                    {
                        DeliveryStatus.Available => "Waiting for a rider to accept this delivery.",
                        DeliveryStatus.Accepted => "A rider has accepted your delivery and is on the way to pick up the item.",
                        DeliveryStatus.PickedUp => "Rider has picked up your item and is en route.",
                        DeliveryStatus.Delivered => "Rider has delivered your item. Please confirm receipt.",
                        DeliveryStatus.Completed => "Delivery completed. Thank you!",
                        _ => "Delivery pending."
                    };

                    <article class="mp-row">

                        <div class="mp-row__img-wrap">
                            @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(order.Item?.ImageUrl))
                            {
                                <img src="@order.Item.ImageUrl" alt="@order.Item?.Title"
                                     class="mp-row__img" loading="lazy" />
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <div class="mp-row__img mp-row__img--placeholder" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                        <rect x="3" y="5" width="26" height="22" rx="3" />
                                        <circle cx="11" cy="13" r="3" />
                                        <path d="M3 23l8-7 5 5 4-3 9 7" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                </div>
                            }
                        </div>

                        <div class="mp-row__body">
                            <div class="mp-row__top">
                                <h3 class="mp-row__title">
                                    @(order.Item?.Title ?? "Item #" + order.ItemId)
                                </h3>
                                <span class="mp-status @statusClass">@statusLabel</span>
                            </div>

                            <p class="mp-row__seller">Seller: @sellerDisplay</p>

                            @* Payment method pill *@
                            <p class="mp-row__pay">
                                <span class="mp-pay-pill mp-pay-pill--@(order.PaymentMethod == PaymentMethod.Wallet ? "wallet" : "cod")">
                                    @if (order.PaymentMethod == PaymentMethod.Wallet)
                                    {
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 3.5A1.5 1.5 0 012.5 2h9A1.5 1.5 0 0113 3.5v7A1.5 1.5 0 0111.5 12h-9A1.5 1.5 0 011 10.5v-7zm10.5 2.5a.75.75 0 100 1.5.75.75 0 000-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <path d="M7 1a6 6 0 100 12A6 6 0 007 1zm.6 8.9H6.4V6.4h1.2v3.5zm0-4.6H6.4V4.1h1.2v1.2z" />
                                        </svg>
                                    }
                                    @payLabel
                                </span>
                            </p>

                            @* Delivery status message *@
                            @if (order.Delivery != null)
                            {
                                <p class="mp-row__delivery" style="font-size: 0.875rem; color: #6b7280; margin: 0.5rem 0;">
                                    📦 @deliveryStatusMessage
                                </p>
                            }

                            <p class="mp-row__date">
                                Ordered
                                <time datetime="@order.OrderDate.ToString("yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ssZ")">
                                    @order.OrderDate.ToString("MMMM d, yyyy · h:mm tt") UTC
                                </time>
                            </p>

                            @* Mark Delivered — only visible when delivery is in Delivered state *@
                            @if (canMarkDelivered)
                            {
                                <form asp-action="MarkDelivered"
                                      asp-controller="Orders"
                                      asp-route-orderId="@order.Id"
                                      method="post"
                                      class="mp-deliver-form"
                                      onsubmit="return confirm('Confirm receipt of this order? This will release payment to the seller.');">
                                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                    <button type="submit" class="mp-deliver-btn">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>
                                        I have received this item
                                    </button>
                                </form>
                            }
                        </div>

                        <div class="mp-row__price-col">
                            <span class="mp-row__price">₱@order.FinalPrice.ToString("N2")</span>
                            <span class="mp-row__price-label">Final price</span>
                        </div>

                    </article>
                }
            </div>
        }

    </div>

    <script>
            (function () {
                'use strict';
                var toast = document.getElementById('mpToast');
                if (toast) {
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        toast.style.opacity = '0';
                        setTimeout(function () { toast.remove(); }, 400);
                    }, 5000);
                }
            }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

       Login and Register set ViewData["HideNavbar"] = true to opt out. *@

--- Views\Shared\_Navbar.cshtml ---
@using System.Security.Claims
@using ThriftLoop.Repositories.Interface
@inject IShopRepository ShopRepo
@inject ICartRepository CartRepo
@inject IItemLikeRepository LikeRepo

@{
    var userEmail = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.Email)?.Value
                        ?? User.Identity?.Name
                        ?? string.Empty;
    var displayName = userEmail.Contains('@') ? userEmail.Split('@')[0] : userEmail;
    var currentPath = Context.Request.Path.Value ?? string.Empty;

    // Check if current user is a Rider
    var isRider = User.HasClaim(c => c.Type == "IsRider" && c.Value == "true");

    // Resolve live shop name for the navbar pill (only for Sellers)
    var shopLabel = "My Shop";

    // Get cart count and likes count for authenticated users
    int cartCount = 0;
    int likesCount = 0;

    var rawId = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.NameIdentifier)?.Value;
    if (int.TryParse(rawId, out var navUserId))
    {
        if (!isRider && User.IsInRole("Seller"))
        {
            var shop = await ShopRepo.GetByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(shop?.ShopName))
                shopLabel = shop.ShopName;
        }

        if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true && !isRider)
        {
            cartCount = await CartRepo.GetCountByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            var likes = await LikeRepo.GetByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            likesCount = likes.Count;
        }
    }
}

<nav class="tl-nav">
    <div class="tl-nav__inner">

        @* Logo - Redirects based on user type *@
        @if (isRider)
        {
            <a asp-controller="Rider" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__logo">ThriftLoop Rider</a>
        }
        else
        {
            <a asp-controller="Home" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__logo">ThriftLoop</a>
        }

        @* Centre navigation - Hide for Riders *@
        @if (!isRider)
        {
            <ul class="tl-nav__links" role="list">
                <li>
                    <a asp-controller="Home"
                           asp-action="Index"
                           class="tl-nav__link @(currentPath == "/" || currentPath.StartsWith("/Home", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__link--active" : "")">
                        For You
                    </a>
                </li>
                <li class="tl-nav__divider" aria-hidden="true"></li>
                <li>
                    <a asp-controller="Sellers"
                           asp-action="Index"
                           class="tl-nav__link @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Sellers", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__link--active" : "")">
                        Sellers
                    </a>
                </li>
                <li class="tl-nav__divider" aria-hidden="true"></li>
                <li>
                    <a asp-controller="Items"
                           asp-action="Index"
                           class="tl-nav__link @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Items", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__link--active" : "")">
                        My Listings
                    </a>
                </li>
            </ul>
        }

        @* ── Right side: My Shop pill + user dropdown ────────────────────────── *@
        <div class="tl-nav__user">
            @if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true)
            {
                @* My Shop pill — only for Sellers (not riders, not admins) *@
                @if (!isRider && User.IsInRole("Seller"))
                {
                    <a asp-controller="Shop"
                           asp-action="Mine"
                           class="tl-nav__shop-btn @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Shop", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__shop-btn--active" : "")">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8 1a2.5 2.5 0 00-2.5 2.5H3.5A1.5 1.5 0 002 5v8.5A1.5 1.5 0 003.5 15h9a1.5 1.5 0 001.5-1.5V5a1.5 1.5 0 00-1.5-1.5h-2A2.5 2.5 0 008 1zm0 1.5A1 1 0 019 3.5v0H7v0A1 1 0 018 2.5zm-2.5 2H4a.5.5 0 00-.5.5v8a.5.5 0 00.5.5h8a.5.5 0 00.5-.5V5a.5.5 0 00-.5-.5h-1.5v.75a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V4.5h-2v.75a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V4.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        @shopLabel
                    </a>
                }

                @* Cart icon — for all authenticated non-rider users *@
                @if (!isRider)
                {
                    <a asp-controller="Cart" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__icon-btn @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Cart", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__icon-btn--active" : "")" title="Shopping Cart">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="22" height="22" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path d="M3 3h2l.4 2M7 13h10l4-8H5.4M7 13L5.4 5M7 13l-2.293 2.293c-.63.63-.184 1.707.707 1.707H17m0 0a2 2 0 1 0 0 4 2 2 0 0 0 0-4zm-8 2a2 2 0 1 1 0 4 2 2 0 0 1 0-4z" />
                        </svg>
                        @if (cartCount > 0)
                        {
                            <span class="tl-nav__badge cart-badge">@cartCount</span>
                        }
                    </a>

                    @* Likes icon *@
                    <a asp-controller="Likes" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__icon-btn @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Likes", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__icon-btn--active" : "")" title="Liked Items">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="22" height="22" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path d="M20.84 4.61a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 0L12 5.67l-1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 7.78l1.06 1.06L12 21.23l7.78-7.78 1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 000-7.78z" />
                        </svg>
                        @if (likesCount > 0)
                        {
                            <span class="tl-nav__badge likes-badge">@likesCount</span>
                        }
                    </a>
                }

                @* User dropdown *@
                <div class="tl-nav__dropdown">
                    <button class="tl-nav__dropdown-toggle" id="userDropdown" aria-expanded="false">
                        <span class="tl-nav__avatar" title="@userEmail">@char.ToUpper(displayName[0])</span>
                        <span class="tl-nav__name">@displayName</span>
                        <svg class="tl-nav__dropdown-chevron" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.23 7.21a.75.75 0 011.06.02L10 11.168l3.71-3.938a.75.75 0 111.08 1.04l-4.25 4.5a.75.75 0 01-1.08 0l-4.25-4.5a.75.75 0 01.02-1.06z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                    </button>

                    <div class="tl-nav__dropdown-menu" id="userDropdownMenu">
                        <div class="tl-nav__dropdown-header">
                            <span class="tl-nav__dropdown-email">@userEmail</span>
                        </div>

                        @* Regular User Dropdown Items (non-rider) *@
                        @if (!isRider)
                        {
                            <a asp-controller="User" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__dropdown-item @(currentPath.StartsWith("/User", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "active" : "")">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path d="M8 8a3 3 0 100-6 3 3 0 000 6zm-4.5 5.5a5 5 0 019 0h-9z" />
                                </svg>
                                My Profile
                            </a>

                            <a asp-controller="Wallet" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__dropdown-item @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Wallet", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "active" : "")">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 3A1.5 1.5 0 012.5 1.5h11A1.5 1.5 0 0115 3v10a1.5 1.5 0 01-1.5 1.5h-11A1.5 1.5 0 011 13V3zm10.5 5a.75.75 0 100 1.5.75.75 0 000-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                Wallet
                            </a>

                            <a asp-controller="Orders" asp-action="MyPurchases" class="tl-nav__dropdown-item @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Orders/MyPurchases", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "active" : "")">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path d="M1 2.5A1.5 1.5 0 012.5 1h3.879a1.5 1.5 0 011.06.44l2.122 2.12a1.5 1.5 0 01.44 1.061V13.5A1.5 1.5 0 018.5 15h-6A1.5 1.5 0 011 13.5v-11z" />
                                    <path d="M9 4.5V1a1 1 0 011-1h3.5a1.5 1.5 0 011.5 1.5v11a1.5 1.5 0 01-1.5 1.5h-4.5A1.5 1.5 0 019 13.5v-9z" />
                                </svg>
                                My Purchases
                            </a>
                        }

                        @* Rider Dropdown Items *@
                        @if (isRider)
                        {
                            <a asp-controller="Wallet" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__dropdown-item @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Wallet", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "active" : "")">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 3A1.5 1.5 0 012.5 1.5h11A1.5 1.5 0 0115 3v10a1.5 1.5 0 01-1.5 1.5h-11A1.5 1.5 0 011 13V3zm10.5 5a.75.75 0 100 1.5.75.75 0 000-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                My Wallet
                            </a>

                            <a asp-controller="Rider" asp-action="History" class="tl-nav__dropdown-item @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Rider/History", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "active" : "")">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path d="M2.5 3A1.5 1.5 0 001 4.5v7A1.5 1.5 0 002.5 13h11a1.5 1.5 0 001.5-1.5v-7A1.5 1.5 0 0013.5 3h-11zm.5 2.5a.5.5 0 01.5-.5h9a.5.5 0 01.5.5v1a.5.5 0 01-.5.5h-9a.5.5 0 01-.5-.5v-1z" />
                                    <path d="M4 8h8v1H4z" />
                                </svg>
                                History
                            </a>
                        }

                        <div class="tl-nav__dropdown-divider"></div>

                        <form asp-action="Logout" asp-controller="Auth" method="post" class="tl-nav__dropdown-form">
                            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                            <button type="submit" class="tl-nav__dropdown-item tl-nav__dropdown-item--signout">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M2 2.75A2.75 2.75 0 014.75 0h5.5A2.75 2.75 0 0113 2.75v10.5A2.75 2.75 0 0110.25 16h-5.5A2.75 2.75 0 012 13.25v-10.5zM8.5 5a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v3.5a.75.75 0 001.5 0V5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                Sign out
                            </button>
                        </form>
                    </div>
                </div>
            }
            else
            {
                <div class="tl-nav__auth">
                    <a asp-controller="Auth" asp-action="Login" class="tl-nav__auth-link">Sign in</a>
                    <a asp-controller="Auth" asp-action="Register" class="tl-nav__auth-link tl-nav__auth-link--primary">Sign up</a>
                </div>
            }
        </div>

    </div>

<style>
    /* My Shop pill — sits between center links and user dropdown */
    .tl-nav__shop-btn {
        display: inline-flex;
        align-items: center;
        gap: 6px;
        padding: 0.4rem 0.875rem;
        border: 1.5px solid var(--color-border, #e2ddd6);
        border-radius: 999px;
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const dropdownToggle = document.getElementById('userDropdown');
        const dropdownMenu = document.getElementById('userDropdownMenu');

        if (dropdownToggle && dropdownMenu) {
            dropdownToggle.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                const isExpanded = this.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
                this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', !isExpanded);
                dropdownMenu.classList.toggle('show');
            });

            document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (!dropdownToggle.contains(e.target) && !dropdownMenu.contains(e.target)) {
                    dropdownToggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                    dropdownMenu.classList.remove('show');
                }
            });
        }
    });
</script>
